


### Basic Physics Lab
   building_physics_lab_0 = { 
      base_buildtime = 210
      show_tech_unlock_if = { is_nomadic_empire = no }
   
      cost = {
         minerals = 60
      }
   
      required_resources = {
         energy = 1.5
      }
      produced_resources = {
         physics_research = 3
      }
      upgrades = {
         building_physics_lab_1
      }
      prerequisites = { "tech_scientific_method" }
   
      potential = {
         planet = {
            is_artificial_planet = no
            any_tile = {
                has_resource = {
                  type = physics_research
                  amount > 0
               }
            }
         }
      }
   
      allow = {
         custom_tooltip = {
            fail_text = "requires_physics_research"
            tile = {
               has_resource = {
                  type = physics_research
                  amount > 0
                     }
               }
            }
      }
      ai_allow = {
         is_slave_tile_or_planet = no
      }
      ai_weight = {
         weight = 10
      }
   }
   
### Physics Lab II
   building_physics_lab_1 = { 
      base_buildtime = 180
      show_tech_unlock_if = { is_nomadic_empire = no }
      is_listed = no
   
      cost = {
         minerals = 120
      }
   
      required_resources = {
         energy = 2
      }
      produced_resources = {
         physics_research = 5
      }
      upgrades = {
         building_physics_lab_2
      }
      prerequisites = { "tech_physics_advanced_19" }
   
      potential = {
         planet = {
            is_artificial_planet = no
         }
      }
   
      allow = {
         custom_tooltip = {
            fail_text = "requires_capital_1"
            planet = { has_at_least_capital_1 = yes }
       }
      }
      ai_allow = {
         is_slave_tile_or_planet = no
      }
      ai_weight = {
         weight = 1
      }
   }

### Supercollider
   building_physics_lab_4 = { 
      base_buildtime = 180
      show_tech_unlock_if = { is_nomadic_empire = no }
      is_listed = no
   
      cost = {
         minerals = 320
      }
   
      required_resources = {
         energy = 3.5
      }
      produced_resources = {
         physics_research = 11
      }
      planet_modifier = {
         tile_resource_physics_research_mult = 0.05
      }
      prerequisites = { "tech_physics_unified_22" }
   
      potential = {
         planet = {
            is_artificial_planet = no
            is_capital = yes
         }
      }
   
      destroy_if = {
         planet = { is_capital = no }
      }
      allow = {
         custom_tooltip = {
            fail_text = "requires_capital_3"
            planet = { capital_building_3 = yes }
       }
      }
      ai_allow = {
         is_slave_tile_or_planet = no
      }
      ai_weight = {
         weight = 1
      }
   }
   
### Holosuite Entertainment Center
   building_holodeck_1 = { 
      base_buildtime = 360
      show_tech_unlock_if = { is_nomadic_empire = no }
      tags = { cultural_building }
      planet_unique = yes
   
      cost = {
         minerals = 300
      }
   
      required_resources = {
         energy = 5
      }
      planet_modifier = {
         pop_happiness = 0.05
      }
      upgrades = {
         building_holodeck_2
      }
      prerequisites = { "tech_physics_computing_40" }
   
      potential = {
         owner = {
            is_borg_empire = no
         }
         planet = {
            is_artificial_planet = no
         }
      }
   
      produced_resource_trigger = {
         modifier = {
            has_valid_civic = civic_virtuoso
            resources = {
               unity = 1
            }
         }
         modifier = {
            has_valid_civic = civic_prophet_2
            resources = {
               unity = 0.5
            }
         }
      }
      destroy_if = {
         exists = owner
         owner = { is_borg_empire = yes }
      }
      allow = {
         custom_tooltip = {
            fail_text = "requires_capital_2"
            planet = { has_at_least_capital_2 = yes }
       }
      }
      ai_weight = {
         weight = 10
      }
   }
   
### Omicron Holo Field Projector
   building_holodeck_2 = { 
      base_buildtime = 720
      show_tech_unlock_if = { is_nomadic_empire = no }
      tags = { cultural_building }
      empire_unique = yes
      is_listed = no
   
      cost = {
         minerals = 500
         influence = 100
      }
   
      required_resources = {
         energy = 10
      }
      produced_resources = {
         physics_research = 5
      }
      planet_modifier = {
         pop_happiness = 0.10
      }
      prerequisites = { "tech_physics_omicron_28" }
   
      potential = {
         owner = {
            is_borg_empire = no
         }
         planet = {
            is_artificial_planet = no
         }
      }
   
      produced_resource_trigger = {
         modifier = {
            has_valid_civic = civic_virtuoso
            resources = {
               unity = 5
            }
         }
         modifier = {
            has_valid_civic = civic_prophet_2
            resources = {
               unity = 0.5
            }
         }
      }
      destroy_if = {
         exists = owner
         owner = { is_borg_empire = yes }
      }
      allow = {
         custom_tooltip = {
            fail_text = "requires_capital_2"
            planet = { has_at_least_capital_2 = yes }
       }
      }
      ai_weight = {
         weight = 10
         modifier = {
            weight = 0
            from = { sector_controlled = yes }
         }
      }
   }

### Polaric Ion Power Station
   building_polaric_ion_0 = { 
      base_buildtime = 120
      show_tech_unlock_if = { is_nomadic_empire = no }
      tags = { power_plant }
      planet_unique = yes
   
      cost = {
         minerals = 100
      }
   
      produced_resources = {
         energy = 8
      }
      planet_modifier = {
         pop_environment_tolerance = -0.1
      }
      prerequisites = { "tech_physics_field_manipulation_117" }
   
      potential = {
         planet = {
            is_artificial_planet = no
         }
      }
   
      allow = {
         AND = {
         custom_tooltip = {
            fail_text = "requirement_not_homeworld"
            planet = {
               NOT = { has_modifier = "capital" }
               }
            }
         custom_tooltip = {
            fail_text = "requires_capital_1"
            planet = { has_at_least_capital_1 = yes }
       }
         }
      }
      ai_allow = {
         has_resource_block = no
      }
      ai_weight = {
         weight = 1
         modifier = {
            weight = 0
            from = { sector_controlled = yes }
         }
         modifier = {
            weight = 0.25
            is_slave_tile_or_planet = yes
         }
      }
   }
   
### Heavy Industrial Complex
   building_industrial_complex_0 = { 
      base_buildtime = 360

      planet_unique = yes

         AND = {

            fail_text = "requires_minerals"

       }
         }

      base_buildtime = 360
      show_tech_unlock_if = { ferengi_fed_members = yes }
      tags = { cultural_building }
      icon = "building_visitor_center_0"
      empire_unique = yes
   
      cost = {
         minerals = 250
         influence = 50
      }
   
      required_resources = {
         energy = 3
      }
      produced_resources = {
         unity = 2
         sr_beetle_snuff_104 = 1.1
      }
      planet_modifier = {
         planet_migration_xeno_pull = 0.25
      }
   
      potential = {
         owner = {
            is_borg_empire = no
            has_swapped_tradition = tr_federation_adopt
            ferengi_fed_members = yes
         }
         planet = {
            is_artificial_planet = no
         }
      }
   
      destroy_if = {
         exists = owner
         owner = { is_borg_empire = yes }
      }
      allow = {
         custom_tooltip = {
            fail_text = "requires_capital_1"
            planet = { has_at_least_capital_1 = yes }
       }
      }
      ai_allow = {
         has_resource_block = no
         is_slave_tile_or_planet = no
      }
   }

### Diplomatic Corps HQ
   building_bureau_2 = { 
      base_buildtime = 720
      show_tech_unlock_if = { is_nomadic_empire = no }
      tags = { cultural_building }
      empire_unique = yes
      is_listed = no
   
      cost = {
         minerals = 500
         influence = 100
      }
   
      required_resources = {
         energy = 5
      }
      country_modifier = {
         pop_happiness = 0.05
         country_resource_unity_mult = 0.1
      }
      prerequisites = { "tech_society_code_431" }
   
      potential = {
         owner = {
            is_borg_empire = no
         }
         planet = {
            is_artificial_planet = no
            is_capital = yes
         }
      }
   
      produced_resource_trigger = {
         modifier = {
            has_valid_civic = civic_prophet_2
            resources = {
               unity = 0.5
            }
         }
      }
      destroy_if = {
         OR = {
         planet = { is_capital = no }
            AND = {
               exists = owner
               owner = { is_borg_empire = yes }
            }
         }
      }
      allow = {
         custom_tooltip = {
            fail_text = "requires_capital_3"
            planet = { capital_building_3 = yes }
       }
      }
      ai_allow = {
         is_slave_tile_or_planet = no
      }
      ai_weight = {
         weight = 1
         modifier = {
            weight = 0
            from = { sector_controlled = yes }
         }
      }
   }

   building_colony_shelter = { 
      base_buildtime = 180
      show_tech_unlock_if = { NOT = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence } }
      planet_unique = yes
      capital = yes
      level = 0
      ai_replace = no
      produced_resources = {
         energy = 2
      }
      planet_modifier = {
         pop_government_ethic_attraction = 0.05
      }
      upgrades = {
         building_capital_1
      }
   
      potential = {
         owner = {
            NOT = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
         }
         planet = {
            is_artificial_planet = no
         }
         planet = { has_any_capital_building = no }
      }
   
      produced_resource_trigger = {
         modifier = {
            OR = { has_non_swapped_tradition = tr_expansion_colonization_fever has_swapped_tradition = tr_assimilation_1 has_swapped_tradition = tr_expansion_colonization_fever_machine }
            resources = {
               unity = 1
            }
         }
      }
      ai_allow = {
         always = yes
         has_resource_block = no
      }
      ai_weight = {
         weight = 1
         modifier = {
            weight = 0.25
            is_slave_tile_or_planet = yes
         }
      }
   }
   
### Planetary Administration - Uses vanilla icon
   building_capital_1 = { 
      base_buildtime = 360
      show_tech_unlock_if = { NOT = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence } }
      planet_unique = yes

      is_listed = no

      }
   
      produced_resources = {
         energy = 4
         unity = 1
      }
      planet_modifier = {
         pop_government_ethic_attraction = 0.15
      }
      adjacency_bonus = {
         tile_building_resource_energy_add = 1
         tile_building_resource_minerals_add = 1
         tile_building_resource_food_add = 1
      }
      upgrades = {
         building_capital_2
      }
      prerequisites = { "tech_planetary_government" }
   
      potential = {
         owner = {
            NOT = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
         }
         planet = {
            is_artificial_planet = no
         }
      }
   
      produced_resource_trigger = {
         modifier = {
            OR = { has_non_swapped_tradition = tr_expansion_colonization_fever has_swapped_tradition = tr_assimilation_1 has_swapped_tradition = tr_expansion_colonization_fever_machine }
            resources = {
               unity = 1
            }
         }
      }
      allow = {
         custom_tooltip = {
            fail_text = "requires_pops_5"
            planet = {
               count_pops = {
                  count > 4
                  limit = {
                    is_colony_pop = yes
                     }
                  }
               }
         }
      }
      ai_weight = {
         weight = 1
         modifier = {
            weight = 0.25
            is_slave_tile_or_planet = yes
         }
      }
   }

      }

      }

      }
      planet_modifier = {

         pop_growth_speed = 0.05
      }

      }
      prerequisites = { "tech_engineering_materials_1439" }

            is_borg_empire = no
         }
         planet = {
            is_artificial_planet = no
            any_tile = {
                has_resource = {
                  type = food
                  amount > 0
               }
            }
         }
      }
   
      produced_resource_trigger = {
         modifier = {
            has_non_swapped_tradition = tr_prosperity_trans_stellar_corporations
            resources = {
               unity = 1
               sr_prosperity_26 = 1
            }
         }
      }
      destroy_if = {
         exists = owner
         owner = { is_borg_empire = yes }
      }
      allow = {
         AND = {
         custom_tooltip = {
            fail_text = "requires_food"
            tile = {
               has_resource = {
                  type = food
                  amount > 0
                     }
               }
            }
         custom_tooltip = {
            fail_text = "requires_capital_1"

### Civilian District
   space_building_arcology_1 = { 
      base_buildtime = 360
      show_tech_unlock_if = { is_nomadic_empire = yes }
      tags = { housing_construction }
      icon = "Suliban_Light_Blue"
      planet_unique = yes
      ai_replace = no
   
      cost = {
         minerals = 200
      }
   
      required_resources = {
         energy = 2
      }
      produced_resources = {
         sr_prosperity_26 = 2
      }
      planet_modifier = {
         pop_happiness = 0.01
         pop_growth_speed = 0.05
      }
      upgrades = {
         space_building_arcology_2
      }
      prerequisites = { "tech_engineering_materials_1439" }
   
      potential = {
         owner = {
            is_borg_empire = no
         }
         planet = {
            is_habitat_planet = yes
            any_tile = {
                has_resource = {
                  type = food
                  amount > 0
               }
            }
         }
      }
   
      produced_resource_trigger = {
         modifier = {
            has_non_swapped_tradition = tr_prosperity_trans_stellar_corporations
            resources = {
               unity = 1
               sr_prosperity_26 = 1
            }
         }
      }
      destroy_if = {
         exists = owner
         owner = { is_borg_empire = yes }
      }
      allow = {
         AND = {
         custom_tooltip = {
            fail_text = "requires_food"
            tile = {
               has_resource = {
                  type = food
                  amount > 0
                     }
               }
            }
         custom_tooltip = {
            fail_text = "requires_capital_1"
            planet = { has_at_least_capital_1 = yes }
       }
         }
      }
   }
